 ‚Äô‚Äô The attempt to stop Tavera coming at a high speed proved fatal for two traffic policemen
 dendi fliover par buudhvaar ko ek taveraa ne do pulisavaalon ko rond diya jisamen head kanstable nihendra kii maut ho gai jabaki doosraa ghayal ho gaya
 The policemen arrested the driver after the chase and registered a case of culpable homicide
 gujarat main chhathi baar bhartiya janata party kii sarkaar ban gai he
 Vijay Rupani was sworn in as the Chief Minister of the state for the second time on Tuesday
 18 disambar ko aae nateezon ne bhartiya janata party ke liye khatre kii ghanti to baja di he
 Since this is the first time in the last 22 years, BJP seats have gone below 100
 chunaav se pehle kai muddon par bijepi sarkaar baikfoot par thi
 Now even after the formation of the government, these difficulties have not reduced
 mukhyamantri pad kii shapath lene ke saath hi vijay roopaani ke liye ye chunautiyaan unka intazaar kar rahi hai
 1
 gaanvon main BJP ko lokapriy bananavijay roopaani or nitin patel ke saamne sabase ahm chunauti rajya ke gramin ilaakon main party kii sthiti ko majboot karne kii he
 The way the party has lost its grip in the rural areas to the Congress in the last elections, the central leadership can do it
 vahiin 2019 ke aam chunaavon ke maddenjar ek baar phir se mukhyamantri ban rahe roopaani or upmukhyamantri nitin patel ko gramin ilaakon ko vikaas ke gujarat model ke daayre main laana hoga
 The party has won the most seats in four big cities of Gujarat in this election
 2
 Reducing the resentment of the Patels In the results of the Assembly elections, the reason for the party being reduced to just 99 seats is considered to be the resentment of the Patels on the issue of reservation
 jis tarah hardik patel or congress party ne prachaar ke dauraan patel samudaay ko bijepi se alag karne kii muhim chhedi he, party alaakaman ko 2019 ke liye khatre kii ghanti sunai de rahi he
 Therefore, by placing Nitin Patel at the helm of leadership along with Vijay Rupani, the party has given responsibility to both to compensate for the loss in the Patel vote bank so that they do not have to face the resentment of the Patel community in 2019
 ise bhi padhein: haar rahe the gujarat, jetali ne lagaaya ye daanv or jeet gaye modi3
 bjp's fort save in 2019 Assembly elections: Increased seats in Congress account has made BJP feel lost in the fort
 jabaki 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaavon main bijepi ne rajya kii sabhi siton par vijay hasil kar pradhanmantri bane narendra modi ko majboot karne kaa kaam kiya he
 But once again, the challenge of Congress's good performance in the assembly elections is to win all the Lok Sabha seats in the state to strengthen PM Modi in 2019
 2014 main party ne congress kaa supada saaf karte hue sabhi 26 siton par paracham laharaaya tha
 In such a situation, if a seat is reduced in 2019, the credibility of the party can be discounted
 4
 Dealing with the already strong opposition in the assembly, Narendra Modi himself was leading the state during three of the last four terms of the BJP government in Gujarat
